persistent(clock_start)?

write_time :- write(system("date")),
	clock_start <<- real_time.

write_stats :- write("CPU Time ", cpu_time, " Seconds"),nl,
	write("Clock Time ", real_time - clock_start, " Seconds"),nl,
	statistics.

load("RULES2/rules_0063.lf")?

write_time?
